***mystiek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:mystiek.html>mystiek</a> (22163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:mystique.html>mystique</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin"><a href = vnd.unilang:latin.html>Latin</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:mysticus.html>mysticus</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μυστικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mustikós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href = vnd.unilang:already.html>Already</a> mentioned <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> Lodewijk Meyer.
</p>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> forms <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:positive.html>positive</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> obsolescent, particularly <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> inflected <a href = vnd.unilang:one.html>one</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> comparative <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> superlative forms <a href = vnd.unilang:are.html>are</a> functioning <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> independent adjectives <a href = vnd.unilang:to.html>to</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:an.html>an</a> increasing extent.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:naakt.html>naakt</a> (1992)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naket</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">naect</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">nakot</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*nakwadaz</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*nogʷós</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:naked.html>naked</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:bare.html>bare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naald.html>naald</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i>, calque <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a>  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Nadelbaum</i>.
